 pradhanmantri manmohan singh is samay vitt mantralay kaa bhi kaamkaaj dekh rahe hai
 Coaching classes and training centers have been brought under the ambit of service tax, but the education of schools, universities and permitted professional courses have been kept separate from service tax
 sarkaar ne is saal ke bajet main seva kar kaa dayera badhaate hue seva kar kii paribhaasha ko vyapak banaaya he

 is saal ke bajet main seva kar kaa dayera badhaane ke saath-saath seva kar kii dar bhi 10 se badhaakar 12 pratishat kar di gai

 Apart from this, funeral services, burial and embalming services have also been included in the negative list
 haalanki, rail maal dhulaai or yatri kiraaye main seva kar lagane ko lekar bhram kii sthiti bani hui he

 is sambandh main unhone patr likhaa he

 ab tak 119 sevaayen 'sakaaratmak suchi' main shaamil thim or unheen par seva kar lagaaya jaataa rahaa

 sevaaon kii nakaaratmak suchi main kuch sarkari or sthaneey nikaayon ko di jane vaali sevaaon ko bhi shaamil kiya gaya he

 tippaniyan Apart from this, services rendered by one lawyer to another lawyer or to an entity having turnover of less than Rs 10 lakh in the previous financial year are also excluded from service tax

 The report will cover all the important aspects laid down by the High Court and they are as follows
 1
 The medical report of the Girl Child Rape Survivors will be prepared by the female doctor
 2
 The MLC report will be given to the guardian of the minor rape survivors
 3
 Psychiatrists should be made available for girl child rape survivors prior to medical examination
 4
 If the investigation report is delayed, the reason for the delay should be recorded in the medical report
 5
 Girl child rape survivors should accompany their parents during the medical examination
 6
 Necessary medical treatment should be given to Girl Child Rape Survivors wherever necessary
 7
 If girl child rape survivors get sexual dysfunction, then the treatment should be included in the report or not
 8
 If a girl child rape survivor is admitted to a private hospital, it should be reported to the nearest police station

 Trump claimed, "hillary Clinton wants the wall
 
 
 hillari clinton ne 2006 yaa uske aasapaas diwaar ke liye ladaai ladi

 baharhaal, hillari clinton diwaar chaahati hai
 
 
 "he alleged that Hillary wanted to grant amnesty
 bihar main ek baar phir bekhauf aparaadhiyon ne nitish sarkaar ke sushasan kii dhajjiyaan udayi or patna ke ek transporter kii goli markar hatya kar di
 The dead body of transporter Dinanath Rai, who is doing business in Transport Nagar of Patna, was found on NH-19 from opposite Hajipur Circuit House
 unako 2 goliyaan maari gai thim
 At the same time, after arriving at the Hajipur Sadar Hospital, the family members of the hospital are in a bad state
 aspataal main parijanon kii cheekh-pukaar sunakar logon kaa jamaavada lag gaya
 Police is currently investigating the case
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki transporter deenanath apane ghar vaishali jile ke gorul sondho se mangalvaar der shaam patna offis ke liye nikle the, lekin der raat unka shav NH-19 par hajipur circuit house ke saamne mila
 Meanwhile, after investigating the case, the police claimed that Dinanath was murdered elsewhere and the body was then thrown in front of Hajipur Circuit House
 SHO abhaya kumaar ke mutabik deenanath raay transport kaa vyavsaay karte the
 He had left for Patna on Tuesday from his home, Goraul Sondho
 unka shavhajipurcircuit house ke saamne se baraamad hua, lekin vanha par khun nahin mila he
 From this it appears that Dinanath was murdered elsewhere and the dead body was later brought there
 mritak ke parijan munna kumaar kaa kahana he ki deenanath ko do goli maari gai
 He used to work as a transporter in Patna
 isse pehle patna kemgadhahospital ke maalik gopal khemka ke bete gunjan khemka kii bhi hajipur main goli markar hatya kar di gai thi
 Gunjan Khemka has a factory in the industrial area of hajipur, he was attacked outside his factory
 bekhauf badmaashon ne unako teen goli maari thi, jisase unki maukey par hi maut ho gai thi
 The miscreants also shot Gunjan Khemka's driver
 gunjan khemka bihar pradesh ke bijepi vyavsaayik prakoshth ke sanyojak bhi the
 Union Road Transport and Shipping Minister Nitin Gadkari accused the former Congress-led UPA government of setting a record of increasing inflation and corruption and claimed that the countrymen were relieved after the Modi government came to power
 gadakari ne shanivaar ko yahaan pradesh kii bijepi sarkaar kaa ek saal puraa hone ke maukey par yojit kaarykram ko sambodhit karte hue kaha ki purv UPA sarkaar ke shashan main mahangaai, petrol, gas, dijal ne saare ricard tod die
 The Congress government set the world record for increasing inflation and corruption
 unhone daawa kiya, ‘centre main narendra modi kii sarkaar aane ke baad mahangaai khatm ho gai or gas, petrol kii daren kam ho gai
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi is working to change the picture of the country
 desh ko bhrashtachar mukt karnaa chaahate he, vikaas se logon ko raahat dena he, ham kisaanon kii takadir badalanaa chaahate he
 Gadkari said against the backdrop of protests by the state Congress on the completion of one year of the BJP government in the state, "some friends have deteriorated, these friends have become unemployed
 There is no need to look at them
" inamen kuch mitron kii haalat to aisi ho gai he ki na bol paa rahe he naa kuch kar paa rahe he
 He said, 'we want to work and there is no shortage of funds
 purvavarti kendra sarkaar ke kaarykaal main kendra or rajya ke bich takaraav ke kaaran rajasthan kaa vikaas nahin ho paaya
 In the coming four years, Rajasthan will reach a new level of development
 ’ kendriya vidyut evam koyala rajya mantri piyush goyal ne rajasthan kii purv congress sarkaar par urja kshetra ko tahas nahas karne kaa aarope lagaate hue kaha ki varsh 2008-2013 main aayi sarkaar ne vasundhara raaje ke netritv vaali pehali sarkaar ke kaarykaal main urja kshetra main kiye kaaryon ko nuksaan pahunchaaya
 He alleged that due to wrong economic policies and mis-management of the former Congress government, the power companies owed seventy thousand crore rupees
 rajasthan kii mukhyamantri vasundhara raaje ne ek saal ke dauraan chunaav or aachaar samhita kii vajah se kam samay milane kaa zikr karte hue kaha ki iske baavjood har varg ko raahat dene kaa kaam kiya he
 He said that the promises he has made will be fulfilled
 dusron kii tarah nahin he jo vaade karke bhul jate he
 Raje said that he has promised to provide employment to fifteen lakh youth in five years and has given employment to forty thousand youth in the first year, now this trend is increasing rapidly
 unhone vipakshi dalon se achche kaary main judne kaa apil karte hue kaha ki vipaksh achche suzav dekar vikaas main bhagidaar ban saktaa he
 Responding to the allegations of discontinuation of free drug scheme and pension scheme by the Congress, he said that we have not stopped these schemes but increased the budget of the schemes
 mukhyamantri ne kaha ki ham yah yojanaayen band karne vaale nahin hai
 While paying homage to the soldiers who were martyred in the attack on Parliament, Raje said that he will take everyone along and create a new Rajasthan
 unhone kaha ki barmer main prastaavit rifinary kaa nirnay kendra sarkaar se rajya ke hisse ke sambadh main baatcheet karne ke baad karengen
 The former Congress government had ignored the interests of the state by taking a hasty decision on it
 rajya ke hiton kii andekhi nahin honen denge
 Input from language bhrashtachar ke gambhir aaropon se ghiri congress nit upie sarkaar chhavi sudhaarney main jute gai he
 The cost of this exercise is 180 crores
 vah is rakam kaa istemaal apane 'bharat nirmaan' multimedia abhiyaan ke liye karne vaali he
 Keeping in mind the general elections, the government on Monday released a series of audio-visual clips as part of its multimedia campaign
 sarkaar kaa daawa he ki in clipon main upie sarkaar kii nau varsh kii nitiyon kii uplabdhiyaan or prabhaav par prakaash daalaa gaya he
 180 crores @ Bharat Nirman In the wake of the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, an advertisement campaign has been launched for which the expenditure of 180 crores has been revealed
 is abhiyaan ke pehle phej (15 din) main 35 karod rupee kharche jaaenge jisaki samiksha ke baad aage kii ranneeti tay hogi
 It is worth noting that before the 2009 Lok Sabha elections, UPA-I spent Rs 100 crore, which was less than the 'india Shining' campaign of NDA
 endie ne saal 2004 main apane 'india shining' abhiyaan ke liye 150 karod rupee kharche the
 The Ministry of Information and Broadcasting said in a statement that 'mile Hum Aaye Mile Hum Hain Jaana Hoon', under the title 'mile Hum Aaye Mile Humne Hain Jaane', written by Javed Akhtar, underscores the need to continue in the campaign so that Ensure that the nation is able to meet the challenges of economic growth and social equity
 adhikariyon ne kaha ki in audio video clip kaa nirdesan ‘parinitha’ se charchaa main aae baliwood film nirmaataa pradeep sarkaar ne kiya he
 These clips will be shown in theaters and TV channels in the coming days
 'india shining' nahin balki bharat kii asli kahanisuchana evam prasaaran mantri manish tiwari kii maane to yah multimedia abhiyaan varsh 2004 ke rajg ke ‘india shining’ abhiyaan se alag he
 Tiwari said, 'it is not' India Shining 'but the real story of India which we are trying to present through these 12-13 initiatives
 ’UPA kaal main hui ‘shant kranti’ kii jhalkadio-video abhiyaan ke bare main tiwari ne kaha ki yah samprag shashan ke dauraan hui ‘shant kranti’ kii ek choti si jhalak he jahaan janata ko soochna ke adhikaar, manaregaa, pradhanmantri gram sadak yojana jaise sansthanik dhaancha yojanaon se jude adhikaron or bhojan kaa adhikaar or nakad antaran laabh yojana jaisi nayi yojanaon ke jariye shashakt kiya ja rahaa he
 How much the Congress will benefit from this campaign will tell the time to come
 lekin vipakshi abhi se centre sarkaar par is bahaane nishaanaa saadh rahe hai
 So critics see the impression of 'india Shining' in it and are doubting its result
 haalanki congress ko puri ummid he ki jo india shining abhiyaan endie ke liye nahin kar sakaa
 That work will be shown by 'bharat Nirman'
 abhiyaan ke jariye vah votaron tak apni baat pahunchane main kaamyaab rahegi
 US President Donald Trump presented a picture of cricket bat and former US President Eisenhower to Pakistan Prime Minister Imran Khan
 trump ne yah tohfa imran ko somvaar ko diya jab vah unase milane ke liye white house pahunche
 Giving this information in the report published in the Pakistani media, Eisenhower has been the only President of America who saw a cricket test match in Pakistan
 apane sambodhan main trump ne cricketer se rajaneta bane imran kii tarif karte hue unhen 'ek mahaan athlete' qaraar diya
 Expressing confidence in Imran's leadership, he said, 'many things are happening for America
 mujhe puraa vishwaas he ki aapke (imran ke) netritv main pakistan ke liye bahut si shandaar baaten hone ja rahi hai
 'let me tell you that while Donald Trump was holding a press conference with Imran in the Oval Office of the White House, he also spoke on the Kashmir issue
 donald trump bole, 'main pradhanmantri narendra modi se do hafte pehle mila tha or hamane is mudde par baat kii thi

 maine kaha kis par to unhone (modi) kaha ki kashmir

 wo (pakistan) muddon kaa hal chaahate hai or aap bhi iskaa hal chaahate hai

 'vahiin, trump kaa kashmir masale par bayaan aayaa to bavaal ho gaya, jiskaa bharat ne bhi munhtod jawaab diya

 pichley vijetavarsh 2012 main in 53 siton par huechunaav main sapako 24 siton par safalataa praapt hui thi

 matadaata or pratyaasheechauthe charan main 84 lakh mahila or 1032 anya samet ek karod 84 lakh matadaata hai

 star prachaarkachauthe charan main vibhinn partiyon ke sheersh netaaon pradhanmantri narendra modi, sapa adhyaksh mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav, congress upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi, party kii star prachaarak priyanka gandhi, basapa mukhiya mayawati, grih mantri rajnath singh samet anek diggajon ne apni-apni partiyon ke paksh main prachaar kaary main puri takat jhonk di
